\begin{Indent}\textbf{ P\+E\+D\+O\+M\+E\+T\+ER D\+A\+TA I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+F\+A\+CE}\par
{\em ~\newline
 }\begin{DoxyCompactItemize}
\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a01338dd8d53d1be2968638e609a89d10}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S8}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_fusion_library_8h_ab54fe709e6a86a32cec96d770a8e69e0}{bsx\+\_\+set\+\_\+stepdetectionopmode}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a579d0b6ef3326502e47ff7d3223e76e4}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+U8}})
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em This A\+PI is used to set the step detection opmode. accel opmode should be enabled to enable the algorithm since it uses only accel data in the algorithm. As the Pedometer algorithm gives event for every change in steps this A\+PI should be called with Opmode = 1.\+By default, Pedometer feature is O\+FF. To enable, this api can be called with param Opmode=1. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a01338dd8d53d1be2968638e609a89d10}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S8}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_fusion_library_8h_ae6de91e6e190e47a58e36b842c699878}{bsx\+\_\+get\+\_\+stepdetectionopmode}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a579d0b6ef3326502e47ff7d3223e76e4}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+U8}} $\ast$)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em This A\+PI is used to get the stepdetection opmode.\+This A\+PI is called to know the step detection opmode is enabled or disabled This A\+PI can be called only when B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+P\+E\+D\+O\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT is ON. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a01338dd8d53d1be2968638e609a89d10}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S8}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_fusion_library_8h_a7ce0974291e0cfa4d5e5799c74aeef21}{bsx\+\_\+set\+\_\+stepeventdetectionopmode}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a579d0b6ef3326502e47ff7d3223e76e4}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+U8}})
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em This A\+PI is used to set the stepeventdetection opmode;B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+P\+E\+D\+O\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT should be ON and internal step detection event will get enable based on this opmode. As the Pedometer algorithm will start detecting the event for every change in steps, this A\+PI should be called with event state = 1. If event state = 0((It will stop detecting the steps the last step count will be stored till system will call the start detection again). \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a01338dd8d53d1be2968638e609a89d10}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S8}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_fusion_library_8h_a8892e305d4174ab3d241310f5360da73}{bsx\+\_\+get\+\_\+stepeventdetectionopmode}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a579d0b6ef3326502e47ff7d3223e76e4}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+U8}} $\ast$)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em This A\+PI is used to get the stepeventdetection opmode; This A\+PI gives the status of step event detection opmode. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a01338dd8d53d1be2968638e609a89d10}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S8}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_fusion_library_8h_a34e2b5a34800082dea0cdba9c29774ee}{bsx\+\_\+get\+\_\+stepdetectionrobustness}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a579d0b6ef3326502e47ff7d3223e76e4}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+U8}} $\ast$)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em This A\+PI is used to get the step detection robustness. The stepdetection robustness will tell the robustness (i.\+e. the steps detected by algorithm in robust or un robust). \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a01338dd8d53d1be2968638e609a89d10}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S8}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_fusion_library_8h_a1647912da14274cca64c0624cc41db82}{bsx\+\_\+get\+\_\+stepdetectionstatus}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a579d0b6ef3326502e47ff7d3223e76e4}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+U8}} $\ast$)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em This A\+PI is used to get the step detection status. This step detection status will Update for every step get detected from algorithm. The status will retain from the last step detection based on the datarate. This A\+PI can be called only when B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+P\+E\+D\+O\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT is ON. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a01338dd8d53d1be2968638e609a89d10}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S8}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_fusion_library_8h_acb070adfa68472ca3c2e30858091ebcf}{bsx\+\_\+get\+\_\+stepcount}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a80ea3e069ccbe6be2e976f53bb37a219}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+U64}} $\ast$)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em This A\+PI is used to get the steps count. The steps will update for every change in valid movements of a user. This steps count will be updated till the next time the system gets reboot. This A\+PI can be called only when B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+P\+E\+D\+O\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT is ON. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\begin{Indent}\textbf{ A\+C\+C\+EL D\+Y\+N\+A\+M\+IC F\+OR D\+I\+S\+T\+O\+R\+T\+I\+ON I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+F\+A\+CE}\par
{\em ~\newline
 }\begin{DoxyCompactItemize}
\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a01338dd8d53d1be2968638e609a89d10}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S8}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_fusion_library_8h_a51c931fb08904e2435505f76af65152d}{bsx\+\_\+set\+\_\+accdyn\+\_\+distdetmode}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a579d0b6ef3326502e47ff7d3223e76e4}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+U8}})
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Sets the accelerometer dynamic detection mode. This A\+PI is used to set the mode of distortion detection based on accelerometer dynamics. It can be made 0-\/$>$1 when accel dynamics should be used for distortion detection and 1-\/$>$0 when it is preferred not to use accel dynamics for distortion detection. This provision was provide for special usecase of coil testing when magnetic field is moved around and sensor is static, in this case the flag should be 1-\/$>$0. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a01338dd8d53d1be2968638e609a89d10}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S8}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_fusion_library_8h_afd5342cc280d13e0ad0bfeea26949930}{bsx\+\_\+get\+\_\+accdyn\+\_\+distdetmode}} (\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a579d0b6ef3326502e47ff7d3223e76e4}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+U8}} $\ast$)

\begin{Indent}\textbf{ Significant Motion A\+PI}\par
{\em ~\newline
 }\begin{DoxyCompactItemize}
\item 
\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a01338dd8d53d1be2968638e609a89d10}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S8}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_fusion_library_8h_a3943d901746f0e508e317fded44851fa}{bsx\+\_\+set\+\_\+significantmotiondetectionopmode}} (B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+U16)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em This A\+PI is used to set the significant motion opmode. Compiler switch constant B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S\+I\+G\+N\+I\+F\+I\+C\+A\+N\+T\+M\+O\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT should be declared and accel opmode should be enabled to enable the algorithm since it uses only accel data in the algorithm. As the significant motion algorithm gives event one time only when motion is detected, after that it is disabled, hence to restart the detection this A\+PI should be called with mode = 1. Note\+: If the library is initialized for the first time with B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S\+I\+G\+N\+I\+F\+I\+C\+A\+N\+T\+M\+O\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT enabled the algorithm is already enabled no need to use set A\+PI. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em This A\+PI is used to get the significant motion detection status once the motion is detected the significant motion is deactivated. algorithm can be activated by calling bsx\+\_\+set\+\_\+significantmotiondetectionopmode A\+PI. \end{DoxyCompactList}\end{DoxyCompactItemize}
\end{Indent}

 }\begin{DoxyCompactItemize}

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Set the heading sensitivity for compass and M4G Permissible values 0 -\/ 5\+: sensitivity mode values of 0 to 5 is defined If sensitivity is “0”, there will be a lowest heading sensitivity but have high stability level. If high heading stability is desired and heading response is not of importance, this value can be set. If sensitivity is “5”, highest heading sensitivity with low stability. If high heading sensitivity is desired and small heading jitter can be acceptable, this mode can be set. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
This file provides an interface to use the functionality of nine degree of freedom software library.

\begin{DoxyDate}{Date}
2013/02/12 created
\end{DoxyDate}
bsxfusionlibrary -\/ nine degree of freedom software library for the processing of the accelerometer, magnetometer and gyroscope sensor data.\+The library supports different operational modes of the sensors. Additionally, the library provides the virtual sensors like compass, imu, 9dof sensors for orientation processing, which uses the sensor fusion algorithm for estimation of the orientation processing or sensor calibration methods.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a01338dd8d53d1be2968638e609a89d10}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S8}} bsx\+\_\+dostep (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structlibraryinput__t}{libraryinput\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Main library process -\/ divided into three process running at different frequency -\/ dopreprocess , docalibration and dousecase. 

dopreprocess -\/ preprocessing sensor -\/ accel , mag , gyro, compass -\/$>$includes conversions to units from lsb and other preprocessing

docalibration -\/ calibration of accel,mag,gyro -\/$>$ includes classical and fmc calibration for mag

dousecase -\/ C\+O\+M\+P\+A\+S\+S/\+M4G , I\+MU , N\+D\+OF processing

{\em libraryinput\+\_\+p} & -\/$>$ pointer to sensor data structure which includes sensor data S32 type and time stamp in microseconds of U64 type \\

Get the sensor switch list for the current working mode. H\+Wsensor\+Switch\+List is a structure of three elements B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+U8 acc,B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+U8 mag,B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+U8 gyro.\+This function gets the status of these three alements for the given working mode.\+e.\+g. if working mode is B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+W\+O\+R\+K\+I\+N\+G\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+M\+A\+G\+O\+N\+LY then acc = 0,mag = 1,gyro = 0;.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a01338dd8d53d1be2968638e609a89d10}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S8}} bsx\+\_\+get\+\_\+version (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structts__version}{ts\+\_\+version}} $\ast$}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get version of the B\+SX Fusion Library. Version is a structure of four element which consists of major, minor, minorbugfix and majorbugfix. e.\+g. major=3, minor=0, minorbugfix =1 and majorbugfix = 0 implies its bsx 3.\+0.\+1.\+0.

\index{BsxFusionLibrary.h@{BsxFusionLibrary.h}!bsx\_init@{bsx\_init}}
\index{bsx\_init@{bsx\_init}!BsxFusionLibrary.h@{BsxFusionLibrary.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{bsx\_init()}{bsx\_init()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a01338dd8d53d1be2968638e609a89d10}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S8}} bsx\+\_\+init (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structinit_param__t}{init\+Param\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This A\+PI initializes the main library process. If the input pointer is N\+U\+LL then it will initialize with default values defined in the library. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em inputparams} & -\/$>$ pointer to acc,mag,gyro specs and usecase config \begin{DoxyVerb}        Inputparam->accelspec : Pointer to accelspec char array that holds settings for particular accelerometer sensor
        Inputparam->magspec : Pointer to magspec char array that holds settings for particular magnetometer sensor
        Inputparam->gyrospec : Pointer to gyrospec char array that holds settings for particular gyroscope sensor
        Inputparam->usecaseconfig : Pointer to usecase char array that holds settings for particular usecase

        Inputparam->accelspec_status holds the status if the spec is error free and not modified from original

        0 -> error in accelerometer spec char array
        1 -> No error in accelerometer spec array and spec corresponds to bma250
        2 -> No error in accelerometer spec array and spec corresponds to bma255
        3 -> No error in accelerometer spec array and spec corresponds to bma280

        Inputparam->magspec_status holds the status if the spec is error free and not modified from original

        0 -> error in magnetometer spec char array
        1 -> No error in magnetometer spec array and spec corresponds to bmm050
        2 -> No error in magnetometer spec array and spec corresponds to bmm150

        Inputparam->gyrospec_status holds the status if the spec is error free and not modified from original

        0 -> error in gyroscope spec char array
        1 -> No error in gyroscope spec array and spec corresponds to bmg160

        Inputparam->usecase_status holds the status if the spec is error free and not modified from original

        0 -> error in usecase char array
        1 -> No error in usecase char array
\end{DoxyVerb}
\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
zero for success, non-\/zero failed 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\em 0} & -\/$>$ Success \\

{\em 1} & -\/$>$ Error \\

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{bsx\_set\_accdyn\_distdetmode()}{bsx\_set\_accdyn\_distdetmode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a01338dd8d53d1be2968638e609a89d10}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S8}} bsx\+\_\+set\+\_\+accdyn\+\_\+distdetmode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a579d0b6ef3326502e47ff7d3223e76e4}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+U8}}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the accelerometer dynamic detection mode. This A\+PI is used to set the mode of distortion detection based on accelerometer dynamics. It can be made 0-\/$>$1 when accel dynamics should be used for distortion detection and 1-\/$>$0 when it is preferred not to use accel dynamics for distortion detection. This provision was provide for special usecase of coil testing when magnetic field is moved around and sensor is static, in this case the flag should be 1-\/$>$0. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mode} & -\/$>$ Enable/\+Disable mode \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
zero for success, non-\/zero failed 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em 0} & -\/$>$ Success \\
\hline
{\em 1} & -\/$>$ Error \\

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{bsx\_set\_compass\_headingsensitivity()}{bsx\_set\_compass\_headingsensitivity()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a01338dd8d53d1be2968638e609a89d10}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S8}} bsx\+\_\+set\+\_\+compass\+\_\+headingsensitivity (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a579d0b6ef3326502e47ff7d3223e76e4}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+U8}}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the heading sensitivity for compass and M4G Permissible values 0 -\/ 5\+: sensitivity mode values of 0 to 5 is defined If sensitivity is “0”, there will be a lowest heading sensitivity but have high stability level. If high heading stability is desired and heading response is not of importance, this value can be set. If sensitivity is “5”, highest heading sensitivity with low stability. If high heading sensitivity is desired and small heading jitter can be acceptable, this mode can be set. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sensitivity\+\_\+val} & -\/$>$ sensitivity mode for compass \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

zero for success, non-\/zero failed

{\em 1} & -\/$>$ Error \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

\index{bsx\_set\_significantmotiondetectionopmode@{bsx\_set\_significantmotiondetectionopmode}!BsxFusionLibrary.h@{BsxFusionLibrary.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{bsx\_set\_significantmotiondetectionopmode()}{bsx\_set\_significantmotiondetectionopmode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a01338dd8d53d1be2968638e609a89d10}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S8}} bsx\+\_\+set\+\_\+significantmotiondetectionopmode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+U16}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This A\+PI is used to set the significant motion opmode. Compiler switch constant B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S\+I\+G\+N\+I\+F\+I\+C\+A\+N\+T\+M\+O\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT should be declared and accel opmode should be enabled to enable the algorithm since it uses only accel data in the algorithm. As the significant motion algorithm gives event one time only when motion is detected, after that it is disabled, hence to restart the detection this A\+PI should be called with mode = 1. Note\+: If the library is initialized for the first time with B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S\+I\+G\+N\+I\+F\+I\+C\+A\+N\+T\+M\+O\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT enabled the algorithm is already enabled no need to use set A\+PI. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mode-\/$>$} & to activate/deactivate motion mode = 1 activate significant motion mode = 0 deactivate significant motion when mode is set to 1, the significant motion initializes to Initial values \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
zero for success, non-\/zero failed 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em 0} & -\/$>$ Success \\
\hline
{\em 1} & -\/$>$ Error \\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a01338dd8d53d1be2968638e609a89d10}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S8}} bsx\+\_\+set\+\_\+stepdetectionopmode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a579d0b6ef3326502e47ff7d3223e76e4}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+U8}}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This A\+PI is used to set the step detection opmode. accel opmode should be enabled to enable the algorithm since it uses only accel data in the algorithm. As the Pedometer algorithm gives event for every change in steps this A\+PI should be called with Opmode = 1.\+By default, Pedometer feature is O\+FF. To enable, this api can be called with param Opmode=1.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a01338dd8d53d1be2968638e609a89d10}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+S8}} bsx\+\_\+set\+\_\+stepeventdetectionopmode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_bsx_library_data_types_8h_a579d0b6ef3326502e47ff7d3223e76e4}{B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+U8}}}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This A\+PI is used to set the stepeventdetection opmode;B\+S\+X\+\_\+\+P\+E\+D\+O\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+RT should be ON and internal step detection event will get enable based on this opmode. As the Pedometer algorithm will start detecting the event for every change in steps, this A\+PI should be called with event state = 1. If event state = 0((It will stop detecting the steps the last step count will be stored till system will call the start detection again).
